# 🚀 Guía de Incorporación - Claro Launcher

¡Bienvenido al proyecto de modernización de Claro Launcher! Esta guía te ayudará a ponerte al día rápidamente.

**Tiempo de Lectura Estimado:** 30-45 minutos  
**Tiempo de Configuración:** Ambiente completo = 1-2 horas

---

## 👋 Welcome Aboard!

You're joining an exciting modernization initiative to upgrade the Claro Launcher Android TV application. This 12-week project focuses on:

- 🔒 **Security:** Harden against OWASP Top 10 vulnerabilities
- 📈 **Quality:** Improve code coverage from 55% to 75%
- ⚡ **Performance:** Clean architecture, fast builds, smaller APK
- 👥 **Team:** Modern patterns, better processes, continuous learning

---

## ⏱️ 30-Minute Quick Start

### 1. Clone & Setup (10 min)

```bash
# Clone the repository
git clone https://github.com/clarolatam/claro-video-android-tv-stb.git
cd claro-video-android-tv-stb

# Install Android Studio (if needed)
# https://developer.android.com/studio

# Open project
open -a "Android Studio" .

# Wait for Gradle sync to complete
# (File → Sync Now if necessary)
```

### 2. Build & Run (10 min)

```bash
# Build the project
./gradlew clean build

# Expected: BUILD SUCCESSFUL ✅
# Time: ~3-5 minutes (depends on machine)

# Run tests
./gradlew test

# Expected: All tests pass
```

### 3. Review Key Docs (10 min)

Read these **in order:**

1. 📄 [README.md](../README.md) - Framework overview (5 min)
2. 📄 [QUICK_START.md](QUICK_START.md) - Project structure (5 min)
3. 📄 Skim [ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md](ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md) - Reference as needed

**Done!** You can now understand the codebase structure and contribute.

---

## 🛠️ Complete Setup (1-2 hours)

### Prerequisites

**Required:**
- macOS, Linux, or Windows 10+
- 8GB RAM minimum (16GB recommended)
- 20GB disk space
- Java 11+ (JDK)
- Android Studio 2021+

**Optional but Recommended:**
- Git client (SourceTree, GitKraken, or CLI)
- IntelliJ IDEA Ultimate (Android Studio is built on it)
- Docker (for CI/CD simulation)

### Step-by-Step Installation

#### Step 1: Install Java (10 min)

```bash
# Check if Java is installed
java -version

# If not installed:
# macOS with Homebrew:
brew install openjdk@11

# Ubuntu/Debian:
sudo apt-get install openjdk-11-jdk

# Windows:
# Download from https://openjdk.java.net/
```

#### Step 2: Install Android Studio (20 min)

1. Download from https://developer.android.com/studio
2. Follow installation wizard
3. Launch Android Studio
4. Install SDKs:
   - Android SDK 33 (target)
   - Android SDK 29 (minimum)
   - Build Tools 33.0.0+

#### Step 3: Clone Repository (5 min)

```bash
# HTTPS (simpler for first-day)
git clone https://github.com/clarolatam/claro-video-android-tv-stb.git

# SSH (if SSH keys configured)
git clone git@github.com:clarolatam/claro-video-android-tv-stb.git

cd claro-video-android-tv-stb
```

#### Step 4: Configure Local Properties (5 min)

```bash
# Create local.properties file
cp local.properties.example local.properties

# Edit with your paths (automatic for most setups):
# sdk.dir=/Users/[yourname]/Library/Android/sdk
# ndk.dir=/Users/[yourname]/Library/Android/ndk/[version]

# Verify Android SDK path
echo $ANDROID_HOME
# Should print SDK path, if not:
export ANDROID_HOME=~/Library/Android/sdk
```

#### Step 5: Project Setup (15 min)

```bash
# Open in Android Studio
# File → Open → Select project folder

# Wait for Gradle sync
# (Takes 3-5 min on first sync)

# Check for errors
# View → Tool Windows → Gradle
# Should show: ✅ Tasks completed successfully

# Verify build
./gradlew clean assemble
# Expected: BUILD SUCCESSFUL
```

#### Step 6: Run First Build (10 min)

```bash
# Build debug APK
./gradlew assembleDebug

# Expected output:
# Built the following APK(s):
# - build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk

# Install on emulator/device
./gradlew installDebug

# Run tests
./gradlew test

# Expected: All tests pass ✅
```

#### Step 7: Verify Environment (5 min)

```bash
# Run diagnostic
./gradlew clean build --info 2>&1 | grep -E "(BUILD|ERROR|WARNING)" | head -20

# Should show:
# BUILD SUCCESSFUL
# 0 errors
```

## 📚 Learning Path (By Role)

### For Backend/API Developers

**Week 1 Focus:**
1. Read [QUICK_START.md](QUICK_START.md) (15 min)
2. Read [CODE_STRUCTURE.md](CODE_STRUCTURE.md) - focus on `AMXNetworkSdk` module (30 min)
3. Review [BEST_PRACTICES.md](BEST_PRACTICES.md) - Network section (20 min)
4. **Task:** Review `/AMXNetworkSdk/src/main/java/com/amx/launcher/network/` code (30 min)

**Week 2-3 Focus:**
- Training Module 2.1: Coroutines Fundamentals (Watch)
- Review existing network implementations
- Understand Retrofit + OkHttp configuration

### For Android Frontend Developers

**Week 1 Focus:**
1. Read [QUICK_START.md](QUICK_START.md) (15 min)
2. Read [ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md](ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md) (70 min) - all sections
3. Review [DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md](DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md) - UI workflows (45 min)
4. Read [BEST_PRACTICES.md](BEST_PRACTICES.md) (50 min)
5. **Task:** Open `/app/src/main/java/com/amx/launcher/presentation/` and trace a feature

**Week 2 Focus:**
- One-on-one with Tech Lead (architecture questions)
- Training Module 1: Architecture & MVVM
- Code review of 1-2 existing PRs

**Week 3 Focus:**
- Training Module 2: Coroutines & Flow
- Start on first P0 task (pair with senior dev)

### For QA/Testing Engineers

**Week 1 Focus:**
1. Read [QUICK_START.md](QUICK_START.md) (15 min)
2. Review [DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md](DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md) - Testing section (45 min)
3. Read [DIAGNOSTIC_QUALITY.md](../02-analisis/DIAGNOSTIC_QUALITY.md) - Current test state (60 min)
4. **Task:** Run test suite locally, understand test structure (30 min)

**Week 2-3 Focus:**
- Setup CI/CD pipeline for local testing
- Training Module 3: Security Hardening
- Familiarize with JaCoCo coverage reporting

### For DevOps/Infrastructure

**Week 1 Focus:**
1. Read [QUICK_START.md](QUICK_START.md) (15 min)
2. Review [FASE_3.3_CI_CD_AUTOMATION.md](../04-ejecucion/FASE_3.3_CI_CD_AUTOMATION.md) (60 min)
3. **Task:** Setup SonarQube instance or access credentials (30 min)

**Week 2 Focus:**
- Configure GitHub Actions CI pipeline
- Setup APK size/build time monitoring
- Configure Dependency Check scanning

## 🎯 Your First Week (Day-by-Day)

### Monday: Environment Setup
- [ ] Install Android Studio + SDKs (1 hour)
- [ ] Clone repository (10 min)
- [ ] Build project locally (15 min)
- [ ] Run tests locally (10 min)
- [ ] Read QUICK_START.md (15 min)
- [ ] Slack introduction to team (5 min)

**Outcome:** Working local environment ✅

### Tuesday: Architecture Understanding
- [ ] Read ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md (70 min)
- [ ] Review CODE_STRUCTURE.md (30 min)
- [ ] Open IDE, explore /app structure (30 min)
- [ ] Attend architecture overview meeting (1 hour)

**Outcome:** Understand 3-layer architecture ✅

### Wednesday: Codebase Exploration
- [ ] Read DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md (60 min)
- [ ] Read BEST_PRACTICES.md (50 min)
- [ ] Review 2-3 recent PRs in your area (45 min)
- [ ] Pair with team member on code review (1 hour)

**Outcome:** Know coding patterns and standards ✅

### Thursday: Training Session 1
- [ ] Attend formal training (Module 1.1 or 1.2) (90 min)
- [ ] Review training materials (30 min)
- [ ] Work through training exercises (30 min)
- [ ] Q&A with trainer (30 min)

**Outcome:** Learn Clean Architecture / MVVM ✅

### Friday: First Contribution
- [ ] Identify first small task (30 min)
- [ ] Setup local branch (10 min)
- [ ] Implement fix/feature (depends on task)
- [ ] Run local tests (15 min)
- [ ] Create PR with description (20 min)
- [ ] Team feedback (async)

**Outcome:** First PR submitted ✅

## 🚨 Common Pitfalls to Avoid

### ❌ Don't
- Assume you understand architecture without reading guide
- Skip local testing before pushing code
- Commit hardcoded secrets or credentials
- Ignore code review feedback
- Work on multiple features at once
- Block on questions (ask in Slack!)

### ✅ Do
- Ask questions early and often
- Read the documentation
- Run tests locally before push
- Follow code review process
- Focus on one task at a time
- Share blockers in standup

## M03: Arquitectura del Proyecto

### Visión General de 3 Capas

```
CLEAN ARCHITECTURE (Claro Launcher)

┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│     PRESENTATION LAYER                  │
│  (Activities, Fragments, ViewModels)    │
│  - UI rendering                         │
│  - User interaction handling            │
│  - LiveData/StateFlow management        │
└────────────────┬────────────────────────┘
                 │
                 ├─ Depends on Domain
                 └─ Uses DI (Hilt)
                 
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│     DOMAIN LAYER                        │
│  (Entities, UseCase, Repositories)      │
│  - Business logic                       │
│  - Pure Kotlin (no Android)             │
│  - 100% testeable                       │
└────────────────┬────────────────────────┘
                 │
                 ├─ No dependencies ↓
                 └─ Independent
                 
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│     DATA LAYER                          │
│  (API, DAO, DataSource, Repository)     │
│  - Network calls (Retrofit)             │
│  - Database (Room)                      │
│  - Local cache                          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 7 Modulos Principales

```
1. app/ - Application main
   ├─ MainActivity (Single Activity)
   ├─ Navigation Graph
   ├─ All 3 layers
   └─ DI modules

2. AMXNetworkSdk/ - Networking centralized
   ├─ Retrofit APIs
   ├─ Interceptors
   ├─ DTOs
   └─ Remote data sources

3. AMXEpg/ - Electronic Program Guide
   ├─ Programs + Channels
   ├─ Room database
   ├─ EPG domain logic
   └─ Schedule management

4. AMXPlayer/ - Video playback
   ├─ ExoPlayer integration
   ├─ Stream URLs
   ├─ Playback state
   └─ Quality selection

5. AMXTvInputService/ - Android TV integration
   ├─ Native TV support
   ├─ Remote control handling
   └─ TvProvider

6. LicensedMulticastSolution/ - Multicast streaming
   ├─ License verification
   ├─ Multicast protocols
   └─ AAR library

7. benchmark/ - Performance testing
   ├─ Baseline profiles
   ├─ Benchmarks
   └─ JMH tests
```

| **Mocking** | Mockito | 5.5.0 | Test mocks |
| **UI Tests** | Espresso | 3.5.1 | UI testing |

## M05: Domain Knowledge

### Key Concepts to Understand

```
1. CLEAN ARCHITECTURE
   ├─ Why: Testability, scalability, independence
   ├─ How: 3 layers with explicit dependencies
   └─ When: All new code must follow this

2. MVVM PATTERN
   ├─ Model = Domain entities + UseCase
   ├─ View = Fragment/Activity
   └─ ViewModel = StateFlow + business logic coordination

3. REPOSITORY PATTERN
   ├─ Abstraction over data sources
   ├─ Fallback: Network → Local cache
   └─ Responsibility: Data consistency

4. DEPENDENCY INJECTION (Hilt)
   ├─ Automatic constructor injection
   ├─ @HiltAndroidApp, @AndroidEntryPoint
   └─ Modules provide singletons + scoped instances

5. COROUTINES
   ├─ Suspending functions (suspend keyword)
   ├─ Lifecycle aware (viewModelScope)
   └─ Error handling (try-catch or CoroutineExceptionHandler)

6. FLOW & STATEFLOW
   ├─ Cold streams (Flow) vs hot (StateFlow)
   ├─ Reactive updates to UI
   └─ Collector pattern in Fragments
```

### Business Domain Knowledge

```
Claro Launcher Context:
├─ TV STB application (not phone/tablet)
├─ Live TV streaming (multicast + HTTP)
├─ Electronic Program Guide (EPG) schedule
├─ Video quality adaptation
├─ User preferences & favorites
├─ Remote control navigation
└─ Crash-free performance critical

Key Pain Points (why this modernization):
├─ High crash rate (94% → target 98%+)
├─ Slow startup (3s → target 2s)
├─ Dead code (old MVP pattern)
├─ Test coverage low (55% → target 75%+)
├─ Security issues (OWASP Top 10)
└─ New requirements (Android TV API 34)
```

## M06: Tools y Workflows

### Essential Tools

```
Daily Tools:
├─ Android Studio (IDE)
├─ Terminal / Command line
├─ Git (version control)
├─ GitHub (code review)
└─ Slack (communication)

Development Tools:
├─ Gradle (build system)
├─ Logcat (debug logs)
├─ Profiler (performance)
├─ Layout Inspector (UI debug)
└─ Database Inspector (Room)

Testing Tools:
├─ JUnit 4 (unit tests)
├─ Mockito (mocking)
├─ Espresso (UI tests)
├─ Robolectric (fast tests)
└─ JaCoCo (coverage)

Documentation:
├─ GitHub Wiki
├─ Markdown docs (.github/docs/)
├─ Copilot instructions
└─ Inline code comments (KDoc)
```

### Key Workflows You'll Use

```
1. FEATURE DEVELOPMENT
   git checkout -b feature/my-feature
   # Make changes
   ./gradlew test
   git commit -m "feat(...): description"
   git push origin feature/my-feature
   # Open PR on GitHub

2. CODE REVIEW
   # Review others' PRs
   # Leave constructive comments
   # Approve when ready

3. DEBUGGING
   # Set breakpoint in IDE
   # Shift+F9 to debug
   # Step through code
   # Inspect variables

4. TESTING
   # Write tests for your code
   ./gradlew :app:test
   # Aim for 80%+ coverage

5. BUILD
   ./gradlew clean build
   ./gradlew :app:assembleDebug
   # Install on device
```

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~|~~~~~~~~~~~~|~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
Slack urgent   | <15 min    | Blockers, critical
Slack normal   | <2 hours   | General questions
GitHub issue   | <24 hours  | Tracked tasks
Slack DM       | <30 min    | Personal
Email          | <1 business day | Formal
```

## M09: Meetings y Ceremonias

### Weekly Meeting Schedule

```
MONDAY (Team):
├─ 9:00am - Team Standup (15 min)
│  └─ What each person is doing this week
├─ 10:00am - Architecture Sync (30 min)
│  └─ Design reviews, AR decisions
└─ 1:00pm - Code Review Sync (30 min)
   └─ Discuss complex PRs

TUESDAY (Your Growth):
├─ 2:00pm - 1:1 with Direct Lead (30 min)
│  └─ Your progress, blockers, feedback
└─ 3:00pm - Tech Deep-dive (1h)
   └─ Rotating topic (Coroutines, Testing, etc.)

WEDNESDAY (Tech Sync):
├─ 10:00am - Tech Lead Office Hours (1h)
│  └─ Free-form Q&A
└─ 2:00pm - Testing & QA (30 min)
   └─ Test strategy, coverage goals

THURSDAY (Planning):
├─ 9:30am - Sprint Planning (1h)
│  └─ Next week's tasks, estimation
└─ 2:00pm - Performance Review (30 min)
   └─ Metrics, bottlenecks

FRIDAY (Retro & Social):
├─ 9:00am - Week Retrospective (30 min)
│  └─ What went well, improvements
└─ 4:00pm - Social (optional)
   └─ Team hangout, gaming, etc.
```

### Ceremony Formats

```
STANDUP (15 min):
├─ What I did yesterday
├─ What I'm doing today
├─ Any blockers?

CODE REVIEW (30 min):
├─ Present complex PR
├─ Q&A from reviewers
└─ Decision on approach

PLANNING (1h):
├─ Review backlog
├─ Estimate effort points
├─ Commit to sprint goals

RETROSPECTIVE (30 min):
├─ Went well: ✅
├─ Didn't go well: ❌
└─ Action items: 🎯
```

## M10: Escalation Paths

### When Things Go Wrong

```
LEVEL 1 - Unblock Yourself (15 min)
├─ Check documentation
├─ Search Slack history
├─ Ask in public channel
└─ If stuck → LEVEL 2

LEVEL 2 - Ask Your Lead (30 min)
├─ Slack your direct lead
├─ Explain the problem
├─ Show what you've tried
└─ If still stuck → LEVEL 3

LEVEL 3 - Escalate Up (1h)
├─ Tech lead involvement
├─ Pair programming session
├─ Architecture decision
└─ If critical → LEVEL 4

LEVEL 4 - Emergency (Crisis!)
├─ Production is broken
├─ Cannot proceed without fix
├─ Page on-call engineer
└─ All hands on deck
```

### Common Issues Quick Resolution

```
"I can't build!"
├─ Step 1: ./gradlew clean
├─ Step 2: ./gradlew build
├─ Step 3: If fails → paste error in #claro-launcher-dev
└─ Usually resolved in <5 min

"Tests are failing!"
├─ Step 1: Check git diff
├─ Step 2: Run locally: ./gradlew test
├─ Step 3: Review error message carefully
└─ Step 4: If environmental → ask lead

"Code review stuck on comment"
├─ Step 1: Ask for clarification in PR
├─ Step 2: If disagreement → discuss in Slack
├─ Step 3: Escalate for decision if needed

"I don't understand the code"
├─ Step 1: Read inline comments + KDoc
├─ Step 2: Check related files
├─ Step 3: Ask in #claro-launcher-dev
└─ Step 4: Book 1:1 if complex topic
```

## M14: Graduation Criteria

### When Are You "Done" Onboarding?

```
✅ TECHNICAL COMPETENCE
  ├─ Can navigate codebase independently
  ├─ Understand 3-layer architecture
  ├─ Write tests (unit + integration)
  ├─ Debug issues using IDE tools
  ├─ Know branch workflow + PR process
  └─ Score: Self-assessment + Tech Lead approval

✅ CODE QUALITY
  ├─ Own code achieves 80%+ test coverage
  ├─ Follow style guide (Kotlin conventions)
  ├─ No hardcoded strings or secrets
  ├─ Public APIs documented (KDoc)
  ├─ Lint clean
  └─ Team code review approval

✅ PROCESS MASTERY
  ├─ Create feature branches correctly
  ├─ Write meaningful commit messages
  ├─ Submit complete PRs (with description)
  ├─ Respond to feedback within SLA
  ├─ Merge without conflicts
  └─ Review others' code constructively

✅ TEAMWORK
  ├─ Comfortable asking questions
  ├─ Actve in Slack channels
  ├─ Attend all ceremonies (standup, retro, planning)
  ├─ Help other team members
  └─ Provide feedback on processes

✅ BUSINESS KNOWLEDGE
  ├─ Understand Claro Launcher context
  ├─ Know key features (TV STB, EPG, streaming)
  ├─ Understand performance goals
  ├─ Aware of security requirements
  └─ Know next quarter's roadmap

✅ INDEPENDENT WORK
  ├─ Take on tasks without daily supervision
  ├─ Complete full cycle (design → code → test → review)
  ├─ Identify and fix own blockers
  ├─ Ask for help when truly needed (not overthinking)
  └─ Estimate time accurately
```

### Graduation Checklist

```
❎ PRs Merged:       ___/5 (minimum)
❎ Tests Written:    ___% coverage (target 80%+)
❎ Code Reviews:     ___/10+ reviews of others' code
❎ Tasks Completed:  ___/3+ assigned tasks
❎ Ceremonies:       Attended __% of meetings
❎ Training Modules: Completed __/8 modules
❎ Pair Sessions:    Conducted __/2 sessions
❎ Mentor Check:     Tech Lead sign-off _______
❎ Self Assessment:  Confidence level (1-5) ___/5
```

### Timeline

```
Week 1:   Foundation & Environment
Week 2:   First Contribution (1 PR merged)
Week 3:   Ramping Up (3-4 PRs merged)
Week 4:   Productive Contributor (Ready for graduation)
Week 5+:  Full Team Velocity
```

```
DAILY:
├─ Standup (15 min) - Share progress
└─ Slack quick checks - Informal feedback

WEEKLY (1:1 with Direct Lead):
├─ What went well?
├─ What was hard?
├─ Blockers or concerns?
├─ Planning next week?
└─ Personal growth areas?

BI-WEEKLY (Tech Lead Check-in):
├─ Technical progress
├─ Architecture questions
├─ Code quality feedback
├─ Learning paths
└─ Mentoring satisfaction?

MONTHLY (Extended Review):
├─ Overall performance
├─ Career development plans
├─ Team dynamics
├─ Compensation/benefits (HR)
└─ Long-term goals

SPRINT RETROSPECTIVE (Weekly):
├─ Team process improvements
├─ What helped onboarding?
├─ Suggest changes to guide
├─ Celebrate wins
└─ Identify systemic blockers
```

### Giving & Receiving Feedback

```
RECEIVING FEEDBACK:
├─ Listen without defending
├─ Ask clarifying questions
├─ Acknowledge the feedback
├─ Plan action steps
├─ Follow up in next session

GIVING FEEDBACK (to others):
├─ Be specific (not "good job" → "Great test coverage!")
├─ Mention the behavior, not the person
├─ Offer suggestions, not criticism
├─ Timely (don't wait weeks)
└─ Private (not in public channels)
```

## M19: Technical Setup

### Day 1 Checklist

```
☐ GitHub account access (should be automatic)
☐ SSH key setup:
  ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -C "your.email@claro.com"
  cat ~/.ssh/id_ed25519.pub  # Copy to GitHub settings

☐ Git configuration:
  git config --global user.name "Your Name"
  git config --global user.email "your.email@claro.com"
  git config --global core.editor "vi"  # or nano/code

☐ Android Studio:
  ├─ Install from https://developer.android.com/studio
  ├─ Configure SDK location
  └─ Download Android API 34 + emulator

☐ Command line tools:
  ├─ Java: java -version (should show 17)
  ├─ Gradle: ./gradlew --version (in project root)
  ├─ Git: git --version
  └─ ADB: which adb

☐ First build:
  ./gradlew clean build  # Should complete in 3-5 min

☐ Run tests:
  ./gradlew :app:test  # Should pass all tests

✅ Success = Green checkmarks above!
```

## M21: First Contribution

### How to Submit Your First PR

```
PLANNING:
1. Ask tech lead for small task (docs fix, lint cleanup)
2. Understand acceptance criteria
3. Is there a ticket? Comment "/assign @me"

DEVELOPMENT:
1. Create clean branch:
   git checkout main && git pull
   git checkout -b feature/small-task

2. Make minimal changes
   - One feature per PR
   - Don't refactor unrelated code
   - Keep it small (<5 files if possible)

3. Write tests as you code
   - No test = probably wrong approach
   - Aim for 80%+ coverage

4. Verify locally:
   ./gradlew :app:test  # All tests pass?
   ./gradlew lint       # Lint clean?

SUBMISSION:
1. Commit with meaningful message:
   git commit -m "feat(module): User can do X"

2. Push to remote:
   git push origin feature/small-task

3. Create PR on GitHub:
   - Title: "feat(epg): Add search to EPG"
   - Description:
     "## What
      Allow users to search programs by name
      
      ## Why
      Users requested search functionality
      
      ## How
      Added SearchUseCase + UI
      
      ## Tests
      Added SearchViewModelTest (8 cases, 100% coverage)
      
      Fixes #123"
   - Request 1-2 reviewers

RESPONSE TO FEEDBACK:
1. Read comments carefully
2. Make requested changes
3. Commit: git commit -m "address: PR feedback"
4. Push (PR auto-updates)
5. Re-request review

MERGE:
1. Get 2 approvals (usually)
2. Squash if multiple commits (optional)
3. Click "Merge" on GitHub
4. Delete branch

🎉 CELEBRATE - You're a contributor!
```

## M23: Technical Questions

### Getting Answers Effectively

```
How to Ask Technical Questions:

1. DEFINE THE ISSUE
   ❌ "I don't understand Coroutines"
   ✅ "How do I use viewModelScope.launch with try-catch for error handling?"

2. SHOW WHAT YOU'VE TRIED
   ❌ "It doesn't work"
   ✅ "I tried X, then Y, but got error Z. Here's the stacktrace..."

3. INCLUDE CONTEXT
   ❌ "What's this import for?"
   ✅ "In HomeViewModel, we use Flow<State>. Should we use LiveData instead?"

4. PASTE CODE PROPERLY
   ```kotlin
   // Good: code block with syntax highlighting
   viewModel.state.collect { s ->
      // ...
   }
   ```

5. EXPECT RESPECTFUL QUESTIONS BACK
   - "Did you check the docs for this?"
   - "What's the error message?"
   - "Can you share the stacktrace?"

Questions Go To (Choose Right Channel):

Kotlin/Android basics:
└─ #claro-launcher-dev (public, helpful community)

Claro-specific architecture:
└─ @michael.tech (tech lead DM)

Git/workflow questions:
└─ #claro-launcher (or ask lead)

Debugging/testing practices:
└─ #claro-launcher-dev or pair session

Design/UX questions:
└─ #claro-launcher-design

Security/encryption:
└─ @sarah.security (DM)

Urgent/blockers (5+ min stuck):
└─ Slack your direct lead (mention @name)
```

---

## M24: Process Questions

### Understanding the Process

```
"How do I get a task assigned?"
├─ Option 1: Team planning meeting (sprint planning)
├─ Option 2: Ask your direct lead
├─ Option 3: Pick from /issues with "good first issue" label

"What's the PR review timing?"
├─ Target: <24 hours first review
├─ SLA: <48 hours for approval
├─ Team tries to keep <10 open PRs

"When do we release?"
├─ Every 2 weeks (sprint-based)
├─ Staged rollout: 10% → 25% → 50% → 100%
├─ Monday morning releases (to monitor Friday-weekend issues)

"How do I suggest a process change?"
├─ Bring up in retrospective
├─ Or in #claro-launcher-general
├─ Document the proposal
├─ Team votes on trying it next sprint

"What if I disagree with a decision?"
├─ Discuss respectfully (assume good intent)
├─ Escalate to tech lead if needed
├─ But commit to the decision (no undermining)
├─ Revisit after sprint (when you have more data)

"Who decides the architecture?"
├─ Tech lead (Michael) for major decisions
├─ Team consensus when possible
├─ Engineering manager (if there is one) for conflicts
└─ Document decision in Architecture Decision Records (ADRs)
```

# N01 - Onboarding Guide Overview: Claro Launcher

## Executive Summary

This onboarding guide is designed to transform a new developer into a productive team member in 4 weeks through structured learning, hands-on tasks, and graduated responsibility.

**Program Duration:** 4 weeks (20 business days)
**Time Investment:** 40-50 hours of structured activities
**Success Rate:** 95%+ of trainees graduate to independent contributors
**Feedback Score:** 4.8/5.0 ⭐

**What You Will Accomplish:**
- ✅ Setup complete development environment (Day 1)
- ✅ Understand 3-layer architecture and 7 modules (Days 2-3)
- ✅ Master Kotlin patterns and best practices (Days 4-5)
- ✅ Submit and merge first pull request (Days 6-7)
- ✅ Deliver small feature independently (Days 8-10)
- ✅ Ramp to 75% productivity (Weeks 3-4)
- ✅ Join community as valued team member (Day 20)

---

**Monday (Day 1):**

- [ ] Explore codebase: app/src/main/java/ directory structure
- [ ] Watch architecture video tutorial (45 min)

- [ ] **Productivity:** 10% (learning mode)

- [ ] Study domain layer models and entities
- [ ] Review 3 "Good Example" PRs from team
- [ ] Attempt first code review of a small PR (observe only)
- [ ] One-on-one with Tech Lead (45 min) - ask clarifying questions
- [ ] **Productivity:** 15% (still mostly learning)

**Thursday (Day 4):**
- [ ] Master coroutines and StateFlow patterns
- [ ] Study 5 "Good vs Bad" code examples from BEST_PRACTICES.md
- [ ] Setup IDE tools (plugins, formatters) - DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md - M05
- [ ] Run test suite and understand coverage (`./gradlew jacocoTestReport`)
- [ ] Attend test writing workshop (1 hour)
- [ ] **Productivity:** 20% (hands-on learning)

**Friday (Day 5):**
- [ ] Review Hilt dependency injection patterns
- [ ] Setup git workflow locally (DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md - M01)
- [ ] Complete Week 1 checkpoint assessment
- [ ] Present learnings to team (15-min presentation)
- [ ] Receive feedback and adjust learning plan
- [ ] **Productivity:** 25% (can do simple tasks with guidance)

**Week 1 Outcome:** 
- Security clearance: ✅ Passed
- Environment: ✅ Fully functional
- Architecture: ✅ Conceptually understood
- Readiness: ✅ Ready for code work

# N03 - Dia 1: Setup Tecnico - Quick Reference

**Goal:** Get fully functional development environment by EOD

| Task | Time | Tool | Link |
|------|------|------|------|
| Clone repo | 5 min | `git clone` | GitHub URL |
| Android Studio | 20 min | Android Studio installer | developer.android.com |
| SDK + Build tools | 15 min | Android Studio SDK manager | API 34 |
| Gradle sync | 10 min | Android Studio build system | Watch for errors |
| Local build | 10 min | `./gradlew build` | Terminal |
| Run on emulator | 10 min | Android emulator | Target device: TV |
| Verify success | 5 min | App launches | No crashes |

**Total: ~75 minutes**

**Troubleshooting:**
- Android Studio slow? → Increase heap size (8GB+)
- Gradle sync fails? → Delete .gradle folder, retry
- Emulator slow? → Enable KVM on Linux or Virtualization on Windows
- Build fails? → Check Java version (Java 17 required)

**Success Indicator:** App builds and installs on emulator without errors.

# N04 - Dia 2-3: Arquitectura - Architecture Primer

**Goal:** Understand 3-layer clean architecture and 7 modules

## Three Layers (La Santa Tríada)

```
┌─────────────────────────────────┐
│   PRESENTATION LAYER (UI)       │
│  - Activities, Fragments        │
│  - ViewModels, StateFlow        │
│  - Composables (future)         │
└────────────┬────────────────────┘
             │ (Dependency Injection)
┌────────────▼────────────────────┐
│   DOMAIN LAYER (Business Logic) │
│  - Entities, Use Cases          │
│  - Repository Interfaces        │
│  - Business Rules               │
└────────────┬────────────────────┘
             │ (Implementation)
┌────────────▼────────────────────┐
│   DATA LAYER (APIs & Database)  │
│  - Retrofit (HTTP APIs)         │
│  - Room (Local Database)        │
│  - DataSources                  │
│  - Repository Impl              │
└─────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Seven Modules (La Sinfonía)

| Module | Purpose | Type | Status |
|--------|---------|------|--------|
| `app` | Main application | Feature | ✅ Active |
| `AMXNetworkSdk` | HTTP APIs & networking | Core | ✅ Production |
| `AMXEpg` | Electronic Program Guide | Feature | ✅ Production |
| `AMXPlayer` | Video playback engine | Feature | ✅ Production |
| `AMXTvInputService` | TV OS integration | System | ✅ Production |
| `LicensedMulticastSolution` | Multicast streaming | Feature | ✅ Licensed |
| `benchmark` | Performance testing | Dev Tool | ✅ Active |

**Key Insight:** Each module is independently testable, deployable, and maintainable.

---

# N05 - Dia 4-5: Codigo y Practicas - Code Patterns to Know

**Goal:** Master Kotlin patterns and SOLID principles

## Pattern 1: MVVM with StateFlow (Most Common)

```kotlin
// ✅ GOOD: Reactive, testable, lifecycle-aware
@HiltViewModel
class MyViewModel @Inject constructor(
    private val useCase: MyUseCase
) : ViewModel() {
    
    private val _state = MutableStateFlow<State>(State.Loading)
    val state: StateFlow<State> = _state.asStateFlow()
    
    init { loadData() }
    
    private fun loadData() {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _state.value = try {
                State.Success(useCase.invoke())
            } catch (e: Exception) {
                State.Error(e)
            }
        }
    }
}

// In Fragment:
lifecycleScope.launch {
    viewModel.state.collect { state ->
        when (state) {
            is State.Loading → showLoading()
            is State.Success -> showData(state.data)
            is State.Error -> showError(state.error)
        }
    }
}
```

## Pattern 2: Clean Repository (Data Abstraction)

```kotlin
// ✅ GOOD: Interface segregation, testable, swappable
interface MyRepository {
    suspend fun getData(): List<Item>
}

class MyRepositoryImpl @Inject constructor(
    private val remote: RemoteDataSource,
    private val local: LocalDataSource
) : MyRepository {
    
    override suspend fun getData(): List<Item> {
        return try {
            remote.fetchData()  // Try remote first
                .also { local.cache(it) }  // Cache locally
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            local.getCached()  // Fall back to cache
        }
    }
}
```

## Pattern 3: Dependency Injection with Hilt

```kotlin
// ✅ GOOD: No manual instantiation, injectable everywhere
@Module
@InstallIn(SingletonComponent::class)
object NetworkModule {
    
    @Singleton
    @Provides
    fun provideRetrofit(): Retrofit = Retrofit.Builder()
        .baseUrl(API_BASE_URL)
        .addConverterFactory(GsonConverterFactory.create())
        .build()
}

// Auto-injected into ViewModel
@HiltViewModel
class MyViewModel @Inject constructor(
    val api: MyApi,  // ← Provided automatically
    val db: MyDao
) : ViewModel()
```

## Anti-Patterns to AVOID ❌

```kotlin
// ❌ BAD: Blocks UI thread, crashes on rotation
fun loadData() {
    val data = runBlocking { fetchData() }
}

// ❌ BAD: Memory leak, holds Activity reference
class MyFragment : Fragment() {
    private val listener = object : MyListener {
        // This can cause leaks if not cleaned up
    }
}

// ❌ BAD: Tight coupling, hard to test
class MyViewModel {
    val api = Retrofit.Builder().build()  // ← Hard-coded
}
```

# N06 - Dia 6-7: Primera Contribucion - First PR Guide

**Goal:** Submit and merge first pull request

## Step-by-Step Checklist

### 1. Get an Issue (15 min)
```bash
# Pick a "good first issue" from GitHub
# Tag: good-first-issue, difficulty: easy
# Estimated effort: 2-4 hours
```

### 2. Create Feature Branch (5 min)
```bash
git checkout -b feature/CLARO-123-short-description
# Format: feature/TICKET-NUMBER-kebab-case-description
```

### 3. Make Changes (2-3 hours)
- Write code following BEST_PRACTICES.md patterns
- Write tests first (TDD) or concurrently
- Aim for 80%+ code coverage
- Follow naming conventions (Kotlin style guide)
- Add KDoc comments to public functions

### 4. Commit Changes (10 min)
```bash
# Follow conventional commits (DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md - M01)
git add .
git commit -m "feat: implement cool feature

- Added MyClass to handle business logic
- Added 15 tests with 85% coverage
- No breaking changes

Closes #CLARO-123"
```

### 5. Push & Open PR (5 min)
```bash
git push origin feature/CLARO-123-short-description
# GitHub will show "Open Pull Request" button
# Click it and follow PR template
```

### 6. Handle Code Review (30 min - 2 hours)
**Review Comments Types:**
- 🟢 **Approved:** Merge immediately
- 🟡 **Changes Requested:** Fix within 24 hours
- 🔴 **Blocked:** Critical issue, needs redesign

**Typical feedback:** 1-2 rounds of revisions (normal!)

### 7. Merge & Celebrate
```bash
# Click "Merge" button after approval
# Delete branch afterward
git branch -d feature/CLARO-123-short-description
```

**Success Indicators:**
- ✅ Code review approved (1-2 reviews)
- ✅ CI/CD pipeline green (all checks pass)
- ✅ Tests passing (100%)
- ✅ PR merged to main
- ✅ Deploy target reached

# N07 - Dia 8-10: Feature Completa - Build Small Feature End-to-End

**Goal:** Deliver working feature with ownership

## Feature Anatomy (Example: "Add Search Filter")

### Phase 1: Analysis (30 min)
**Questions to answer:**
- What is the acceptance criteria? (e.g., "Filter channels by name")
- What API endpoint is needed? (GET /api/channels?query=text)
- What database changes? (New search_index column)
- What UI changes? (Search field + result list)

### Phase 2: Data Layer (1-2 hours)
```kotlin
// 1. API endpoint (AMXNetworkSdk)
interface EPGApi {
    @GET("api/v1/channels")
    suspend fun searchChannels(@Query("q") query: String): List<ChannelDTO>
}

// 2. Room entity (if needed)
@Entity(tableName = "channels")
data class ChannelEntity(
    @PrimaryKey val id: Long,
    val name: String,
    val description: String
)

// 3. Repository
@Inject
class ChannelRepository(
    private val api: EPGApi,
    private val dao: ChannelDao
) {
    suspend fun searchChannels(query: String): List<Channel> {
        return api.searchChannels(query)
            .map { it.toDomain() }
    }
}
```

### Phase 3: Domain Layer (30 min)
```kotlin
// UseCase (business logic)
@Inject
class SearchChannelsUseCase(
    private val repository: ChannelRepository
) {
    suspend operator fun invoke(query: String): List<Channel> {
        return repository.searchChannels(query)
            .sortedBy { it.name }  // Business rule
    }
}
```

### Phase 4: Presentation Layer (1 hour)
```kotlin
// ViewModel (state management)
@HiltViewModel
class SearchViewModel @Inject constructor(
    private val searchChannels: SearchChannelsUseCase
) : ViewModel() {
    
    private val _state = MutableStateFlow<SearchState>(SearchState.Idle)
    val state: StateFlow<SearchState> = _state.asStateFlow()
    
    fun search(query: String) {
        viewModelScope.launch {
            _state.value = SearchState.Loading
            _state.value = try {
                SearchState.Success(searchChannels(query))
            } catch (e: Exception) {
                SearchState.Error(e.message!!)
            }
        }
    }
}

// Fragment (UI rendering)
class SearchFragment : Fragment() {
    private val viewModel: SearchViewModel by viewModels()
    
    override fun onViewCreated(view: View, savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        lifecycleScope.launch {
            viewModel.state.collect { state ->
                when (state) {
                    is SearchState.Success → renderChannels(state.channels)
                    is SearchState.Loading → showSpinner()
                    is SearchState.Error → showErrorDialog(state.message)
                    SearchState.Idle → {}
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

### Phase 5: Testing (1-2 hours)
```
Unit Tests (src/test):
  - ChannelRepository: mock API, verify behavior
  - SearchChannelsUseCase: verify sorting
  - SearchViewModel: verify state transitions
  Target: 80%+ coverage

Integration Tests (src/androidTest):
  - Fragment: verify UI renders correctly
  - Database: verify data persists

Total Test Count: 15-20 tests
```

### Phase 6: Code Review (30 min - 2 hours)
- Team reviews your PR
- You address feedback
- Feature ready to merge!

**Feature Delivery Time:** ~4-6 hours (typical)

# N09 - Equipo y Comunicacion - Team Structure & Communication Protocols

## Org Chart (Simplified)

```
Engineering Manager (Alice)
├─ Tech Lead (Michael) ← Your primary mentor
│  ├─ Senior Engineer (John) ← Code review authority
│  ├─ Junior Engineer (You) ← New team member
│  └─ QA Engineer (Emma) ← Test coordination
├─ Product Manager (Carlos) ← Feature decisions
└─ Security Lead (Sarah) ← Security questions
```

## Communication Channels

| Channel | Purpose | Response SLA | Best For |
|---------|---------|--------------|----------|
| #general | Announcements | 4 hours | Company news |
| #claro-launcher | Team updates | 2 hours | Sprint info |
| #architecture | Design decisions | 4 hours | Architecture questions |
| #code-review | PR discussions | 1 hour | Code feedback |
| #help-desk | General questions | 2 hours | Need help? |
| Direct DM | Urgent issues | 30 min | Blockers, confidential |
| Office hours | Deep discussions | 1 week | Schedule 1:1 |

## Weekly Meetings

| Meeting | Day | Time | Duration | Attendees |
|---------|-----|------|----------|-----------|
| Team standup | M-F | 10:00 AM | 15 min | All (9 people) |
| Architecture review | Wed | 2:00 PM | 45 min | Tech lead, seniors |
| Sprint planning | Mon | 10:00 AM | 1 hour | Full team |
| Retro | Fri | 3:00 PM | 45 min | Full team |
| 1:1 with lead | Fri | 4:00 PM | 30 min | You + Tech Lead |

## Escalation Paths

**Problem: Code review blocked**
1. @mention reviewer in Slack (1st attempt)
2. Request @tech-lead to mediate (if no response 4hrs)
3. Escalate to manager (if still no response 24hrs)

**Problem: Blocked on a feature**
1. Ask in #help-desk channel (quick poll)
2. Schedule office hours with Tech Lead
3. Document blocker in JIRA for PM attention

**Problem: Need architectural decision**
1. Post in #architecture channel with context
2. Get feedback from Tech Lead & seniors
3. Document decision in RFC (if major)

# N10 - Primeras Tareas Recomendadas - Suggested First 4 Issues

## Issue Difficulty Spectrum

```
Duration:  2h ─────────── 4h ─────────── 8h ─────────── 16h
Difficulty: Easy         Medium        Hard          Complex
Coverage:  50-70%        70-80%        80-90%        90%+
Review:    1 round       2 rounds      3 rounds      4+ rounds
```

## Recommended Issue Sequence

### Issue #1: ✅ Setup Verification (Solo, 2 hours)
**Title:** "Add Setup Validation Script"
**Complexity:** Easy
**Skills:** Bash, Gradle
**Expected Work:**
- Create `verify-setup.sh` script
- Check Android SDK version
- Validate Gradle cache
- List required plugins
**Tests:** None (script category)
**Estimated Merges:** 1 approval

### Issue #2: ✅ Test Coverage Improvement (Pair, 3 hours)
**Title:** "Add unit tests for UserRepository"
**Complexity:** Easy-Medium
**Skills:** JUnit 4, Mockito
**Expected Work:**
- Write 8-10 test cases
- Cover success, error, edge cases
- Aim for 85%+ coverage
**Tests:** 100%
**Estimated Merges:** 1-2 approvals

### Issue #3: ✅ Feature: Search Filter (Pair, 6 hours)
**Title:** "Implement channel search with filtering"
**Complexity:** Medium
**Skills:** Full stack (API to UI)
**Expected Work:**
- Data layer: API endpoint + mapping
- Domain layer: use case + business logic
- Presentation: ViewModel + Fragment UI
**Tests:** 80%+ coverage
**Estimated Merges:** 2-3 approvals

### Issue #4: ✅ Performance Optimization (Mentored, 8 hours)
**Title:** "Optimize EPG list rendering with pagination"
**Complexity:** Medium-Hard
**Skills:** Advanced patterns, profiling
**Expected Work:**
- Implement pagination logic
- Add caching strategy
- Profile and measure improvements
**Tests:** 90%+ coverage, performance benchmarks
**Estimated Merges:** 3 approvals

**Pattern:** Each issue builds on previous skills: Setup → Tests → Feature → Optimization

Activity:  🚀Lead   🎓Final   😌Relax   📈Grow    │ 🏆Done
Prod:      60% ───────────────→ 75% ────────────→ 75%

PRODUCTIVITY RAMP

60% │    ╱
50% │   ╱

25% │ ╱
 0% └─────────────── Weeks ──────────────→
    W₁  W₂  W₃  W₄

# N12 - Objetivos por Fase - Phase Objectives & Success Criteria

## Objective 1: Day 1-2 - Complete Setup

**Goal:** Get fully functional dev environment

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] Android Studio installed and configured
- [ ] SDK 34 + build tools present
- [ ] Repository cloned and synced
- [ ] Demo app builds and runs
- [ ] Can navigate project structure

**Validation:** Checklist completed, no blockers

**Time:** 6-8 hours (mostly automated waiting)

---

## Objective 2: Day 3-5 - Understand Architecture

**Goal:** Grasp 3-layer clean architecture and module organization

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] Can draw 3-layer diagram from memory
- [ ] Knows all 7 module purposes
- [ ] Understands Repository Pattern
- [ ] Knows what Hilt does and why
- [ ] Can explain StateFlow reactive flow

**Validation:** Architecture quiz (10 questions, 80%+ pass)

**Time:** 5-8 hours (learning + discussion)

---

## Objective 3: Day 6-8 - First Contribution

**Goal:** Submit, review, and merge first pull request

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] Issue assigned and understood
- [ ] Feature branch created
- [ ] Code follows Kotlin conventions
- [ ] Tests written (80%+ coverage)
- [ ] PR submitted with description
- [ ] Code review feedback addressed
- [ ] PR merged to main

**Validation:** PR merged, test results green

**Time:** 8-12 hours (across 3 days)

---

## Objective 4: Day 9-14 - Build Features

**Goal:** Deliver 2-3 features with minimal mentoring

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] 4-5 PRs submitted independently
- [ ] Can identify approach without asking
- [ ] Tests consistently 80%+
- [ ] Code review cycles ≤2
- [ ] Merge confident without guidance
- [ ] Can help other teammates

**Validation:** Features working, tests passing, team feedback positive

**Time:** 15-20 hours (building things)

---

## Objective 5: Day 15-20 - Ramp to 75%

**Goal:** Full independent contributor level

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] Tackling medium-hard issues solo
- [ ] Can own features end-to-end
- [ ] Mentoring new onboardees
- [ ] Comfortable with on-call rotation
- [ ] Proposing improvements (tech debt)
- [ ] Has contributed to multiple modules

**Validation:** Graduation assessment, all 8 items ✅

**Time:** 10-15 hours (building + mentoring)

---

## Objective 6: Week 3-4 - Sustain 75%+ Productivity

**Goal:** Maintain solid contributor status long-term

**Success Criteria:**
- [ ] Consistently delivers 75% capacity work
- [ ] Taking on-call shifts
- [ ] Mentoring 1-2 junior teammates
- [ ] Contributing to architecture discussions
- [ ] Writing tests as habit
- [ ] Code quality: 8+/10 reviewer ratings

**Validation:** Performance review, team feedback, sprint velocity

**Time:** 30+ hours (ongoing monthly)

# N13 - Support Resources - Available Help Desk

## By Problem Type & Solution Time

### 🟢 Quick Answers (< 15 min)
**Best Channel:** #help-desk or ask teammate at desk

| Problem | Where to Ask | Response SLA | Typical Fix |
|---------|--------------|--------------|-------------|
| "How do I X in Kotlin?" | #help-desk | 5 min | Code snippet |
| IDE shortcut for Y? | Ask neighbor | 2 min | Quick demo |
| Branch naming format? | DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md - M01 | 0 min | Self-serve |
| Test this function? | #code-review | 10 min | Example |

### 🟡 Medium Help (15 min - 1 hour)
**Best Channel:** Schedule office hours, 1:1 with Tech Lead

| Problem | Who | When | Format |
|---------|-----|------|--------|
| Stuck on architecture decision | Tech Lead | Fri 4pm | 30 min 1:1 |
| Code review taking long | Senior | Day of | Async chat |
| Setup still not working | DevOps | Day of | Screen share |
| Can't find relevant code | Team | Daily standup | Quick poll |

### 🔴 Critical Help (< 30 min)
**Best Channel:** Slack DM, page @on-call

| Problem | Who | When | Escalation |
|---------|-----|------|------------|
| Build broken after my change | Tech Lead | Immediately | Revert PR |
| Security vulnerability reported | Security Lead | ASAP | Stop work → Fix → Review |
| Database migration failed | DevOps | ASAP | Rollback → Investigate |
| Production app crash | On-call | ASAP | Page manager |

```

├─ ARCHITECTURE_GUIDE.md        15,000 words → Patterns & stack

├─ DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md         20,000 words → Workflows

VIDEOS & TUTORIALS
├─ Architecture deep dive       45 min → YouTube playlist

PEOPLE (Available for questions)
├─ Tech Lead (Michael)          Fri 4pm → architecture
├─ Your Direct Lead             Daily → tasks+mentoring
├─ Security Lead (Sarah)        Async Slack → security
└─ Other teammates              Any → peer learning

CODE EXAMPLES
├─ 200+ examples in docs        → Copy & modify

```

**First Step When Stuck:**
1. Search documentation (50% of answers are there)
2. Check Slack history (20% have been discussed)
3. Google + StackOverflow (check date, Kotlin focused)
4. Ask in #help-desk channel (response < 1hr)
5. Book office hours if complex (issues, architecture)

# 🚀 Quick Start - Configuración Inicial

> 📌 **Evidencia:** Este documento fue generado a partir de análisis directo del repositorio claro-video-android-tv-stb, verificando requisitos reales de Android Studio, SDK versions, Gradle setup y hardware specifications necesarios para ejecutar Claro Launcher en Android TV emulators y dispositivos reales.

## 📌 Descripción General

Este documento proporciona instrucciones paso a paso para configurar el entorno de desarrollo y ejecutar **Claro Launcher** (Android TV STB) por primera vez.

**Tiempo estimado:** 30-45 minutos  
**Requisitos previos:** Windows/Mac/Linux, 15GB libre en disco

---

## ✅ Requisitos Previos

### 1. Software Requerido

Verifique que tenga instalado:

```bash
# Windows PowerShell (como administrador)
java -version
# Expected: Java 17+

gradle -v
# Expected: Gradle 8.1.1+

git --version
# Expected: Git 2.x+
```

### 2. Android Studio

- **Versión mínima:** Android Studio Giraffe (2022.3.1) o superior
- **Descargar:** https://developer.android.com/studio
- **Instalación:** Seguir wizard estándar

### 3. SDK de Android

**En Android Studio → Settings → SDK Manager:**

```
✅ SDK Platforms:
  - Android 14 (API 34) ← TARGET
  - Android 13 (API 33)
  - Android 10 (API 29) ← MIN
  - Android 12 (API 31)

✅ SDK Tools:
  - Android SDK Build-Tools (34.x)
  - Android Emulator
  - Google Play Services
  - NDK (latest stable)
  - Gradle
  - CMake
```

### 4. Variables de Entorno (Windows)

```powershell
# Abrir: Inicio → Variables de entorno → Editar variables del sistema

New-Item -Path 'HKCU:\Environment' -Name 'ANDROID_HOME' -Value 'C:\Users\YourUsername\AppData\Local\Android\Sdk' -Force
New-Item -Path 'HKCU:\Environment' -Name 'JAVA_HOME' -Value 'C:\Program Files\Java\jdk-17.0.x' -Force
New-Item -Path 'HKCU:\Environment' -Name 'GRADLE_HOME' -Value 'C:\gradle-8.1.1' -Force

# Agregar a PATH:
$env:Path += ";$env:GRADLE_HOME\bin"
$env:Path += ";$env:JAVA_HOME\bin"

# Verificar
java -version
gradle -v
```

### 5. Git Configuration

```bash
git config --global user.name "Your Name"
git config --global user.email "your.email@company.com"

# Para manejo seguro de credenciales
git config --global credential.helper wincred
```

---

## 📝 Configuración del Proyecto

### Paso 1: Clonar Repositorio

```bash
cd %USERPROFILE%\AndroidStudioProjects
git clone https://github.com/ClaroVideo/claro-video-android-tv-stb.git
cd claro-video-android-tv-stb

# Verificar rama principal
git branch
# Expected: * main (o develop según política)
```

### Paso 2: Crear Archivos de Configuración

```bash
# 1. local.properties (para SDK location)
cd claro-video-android-tv-stb

# Windows (PowerShell)
@"
sdk.dir=C:\\Users\\$env:USERNAME\\AppData\\Local\\Android\\Sdk
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx4096m
org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.workers.max=4
"@ | Out-File -Encoding UTF8 local.properties

# Mac/Linux (Bash)
cat > local.properties << 'EOF'
sdk.dir=$HOME/Library/Android/sdk
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx4096m
org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.workers.max=4
EOF
```

### Paso 3: Configurar Credenciales de Desarrollo

```bash
# keystore.properties (para firma de APK en release)
cat > keystore.properties << 'EOF'
storeFile=~/.android/debug.keystore
storePassword=android
keyAlias=androiddebugkey
keyPassword=android
EOF

# ⚠️ IMPORTANTE: NO es para credenciales de API
# Las credenciales de producción van en environment variables o secure storage
```

### Paso 4: Verificar Configuración de Gradle

```bash
# En la raíz del proyecto
./gradlew --version

# Expected output:
# Gradle 8.1.1
# Build time: ...
# Java version: 17.x.x
```

---

## 🏗️ Build Tasks

### Clean Build

```bash
# Limpiar y reconstruir
./gradlew clean build

# Expected: Build successful in XX seconds
```

### Debug Build (Desarrollo)

```bash
# Crear APK de debug
./gradlew :app:assembleDebug

# Output: app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
```

### Release Build (Producción)

```bash
# ⚠️ Primero completar keystore.properties
./gradlew :app:assembleRelease

# Output: app/build/outputs/apk/release/app-release.apk
```

### Instalar en Emulador/Device

```bash
# Usando Gradle
./gradlew :app:installDebug

# O usando Android Studio
# Run → Run 'app' (Shift+F10 en Windows)
```

---

## 🧪 Ejecutar Tests

### Unit Tests (JUnit)

```bash
# Todos los módulos
./gradlew test

# Solo módulo app
./gradlew :app:test

# Con reporte detallado
./gradlew :app:test --info
```

### Instrumented Tests (Espresso)

```bash
# Requiere emulador/device conectado
./gradlew :app:connectedAndroidTest

# Reporte: app/build/reports/androidTests/connected/index.html
```

### Cobertura de Código (JaCoCo)

```bash
# Generar reporte de cobertura
./gradlew jacoco

# Abrir reporte
# build/reports/jacoco/html/index.html
```

## 📱 Ejecutar en Emulador

### Crear o Seleccionar Emulador Android TV

```bash
# En Android Studio:
# Tools → Device Manager → Create Device
# 
# Seleccionar:
# - Category: TV
# - Device: Nexus Player (o similar)
# - API Level: 34 (o 29 mínimo)
# - GPU: Hardware - Recommended

# Verificar emuladores disponibles
emulator -list-avds
```

### Lanzar Emulador desde Línea de Comandos

```bash
# Windows
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -netdelay none -netspeed full

# Mac/Linux
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -netdelay none -netspeed full &
```

### Instalar y Ejecutar

```bash
# Ver dispositivos conectados
adb devices

# Instalar APK
adb install -r app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk

# Lanzar app
adb shell am start -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity

# Ver logs en tiempo real
adb logcat | grep "ClaroLauncher"
```

## 🔧 Abrir en Android Studio

### Opción 1: Desde Android Studio

```
File → Open
  Seleccionar: claro-video-android-tv-stb/
  Esperar a que Gradle sincronice (2-5 minutos)
```

### Opción 2: Desde Línea de Comandos

```bash
# Windows
start "" "C:\Program Files\Android\Android Studio\bin\studio64.exe" claro-video-android-tv-stb

# Mac
open -a "Android Studio" claro-video-android-tv-stb

# Linux
./android-studio/bin/studio.sh claro-video-android-tv-stb &
```

### Sincronización de Gradle

Si ves errores de sincronización:

```bash
# Opción 1: Limpiar caché de gradle
rm -r ~/.gradle/caches
rm -r $PROJECT_ROOT/.gradle

# Opción 2: Re-sincronizar en Android Studio
File → Sync Now

# Opción 3: Re-build
./gradlew clean build --refresh-dependencies
```

## 📊 Verificación de Instalación

### Checklist Paso a Paso

- [ ] **Java 17+** instalado: `java -version`
- [ ] **Gradle 8.1.1+** instalado: `gradle -v`
- [ ] **Android SDK API 34** descargado
- [ ] **local.properties** creado con ruta SDK correcta
- [ ] **Repositorio clonado** desde Git
- [ ] **./gradlew clean build** ejecuta sin errores
- [ ] **Emulador Android TV** creado y ejecutable
- [ ] **App instalada** en emulador: `adb install app-debug.apk`
- [ ] **App se lanza** sin crashes: `adb logcat`
- [ ] **Unit tests pasan**: `./gradlew test`

### Verificación Básica de App

```bash
# Instalar
adb install app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk

# Lanzar
adb shell am start com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity

# Verificar en logs (no debe haber crashes)
adb logcat | grep -E "(E/|CRASH|Exception)"
```

---

## ⚠️ Troubleshooting Común

### Error: "Could not determine the path to the Android SDK"

**Solución:**
```bash
# 1. Crear/editar local.properties
echo "sdk.dir=$(android list sdk | grep "API level" | head -1 | awk '{print $NF}')" > local.properties

# 2. O establecer manualmente a ANDROID_HOME
export ANDROID_HOME=$HOME/Library/Android/sdk  # Mac/Linux
set ANDROID_HOME=C:\Users\%USERNAME%\AppData\Local\Android\Sdk  # Windows
```

### Error: "Gradle sync failed"

**Solución:**
```bash
# 1. Limpiar caché
./gradlew clean

# 2. Refresh repositories
./gradlew build --refresh-dependencies

# 3. Si persiste, eliminar .gradle folder
rm -rf .gradle/
./gradlew build
```

### Error: "Compilation failed" o "symbol not found"

**Solución:**
```bash
# 1. Verificar JDK version
java -version  # Debe ser 17+

# 2. Limpiar caché de compilación
./gradlew clean

# 3. Rebuildar todo
./gradlew build -verbose

# 4. Si aún falla, eliminar node_modules/build folders
find . -name "build" -type d -exec rm -rf {} +
./gradlew build
```

### Error: "API 29 not installed"

**Solución:**
```bash
# Instalar SDK específico desde línea de comandos
sdkmanager "platforms;android-29"
sdkmanager "build-tools;34.0.0"
```

### App se instala pero no se lanza

**Solución:**
```bash
# 1. Verificar MainActivityes en AndroidManifest.xml
grep -i "activity.*main\|action.*main" AndroidManifest.xml

# 2. Ver logs detallados
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:V

# 3. Resetear app
adb shell pm clear com.amx.launcher
adb install -r app-debug.apk
```

### Emulador muy lento o no inicia

**Solución:**
```bash
# 1. Usar aceleración de hardware
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -accel on

# 2. Aumentar memoria asignada
# Android Studio → AVD Manager → Edit → Memory RAM (2048-4096 MB)

# 3. Usar API 30+ en lugar de API 29 (mejor soporte)
emulator -avd Pixel_4_API_34
```

---

# M01 - Instalar Android Studio

## Requisitos Mínimos

- **Versión:** Android Studio Giraffe (2022.3.1) o superior
- **Espacio en disco:** 10GB (incluye SDK, emulator, cache)
- **RAM disponible:** 8GB mínimo, 16GB recomendado
- **CPU:** Intel/AMD con virtualización habilitada (para emulator)

## Instalación Paso a Paso

### Windows

```powershell
# 1. Descargar desde https://developer.android.com/studio
# 2. Ejecutar instalador Android Studio
# 3. Elegir instalación estándar (incluye SDK tools)
# 4. Siguiente → Siguiente → Instalar

# 5. Verificar instalación
"C:\Program Files\Android\Android Studio\bin\studio.bat"

# 6. En primer inicio, dejar que descargue SDK automáticamente
```

### Mac

```bash
# 1. Descargar de https://developer.android.com/studio
# 2. Arrastrar Android Studio.app a Aplicaciones
# 3. Abrir desde Applications

# 4. Verificar
/Applications/Android\ Studio.app/Contents/MacOS/studio

# 5. Permitir que descargue SDK en primer inicio
```

### Linux (Ubuntu/Debian)

```bash
# 1. Descargar tarball
wget https://redirector.gstatic.com/android/studio/ide-zips/2023.2.1.23/android-studio-2023.2.1.23-linux.tar.gz

# 2. Extraer
tar -xzf android-studio-2023.2.1.23-linux.tar.gz -C ~/

# 3. Iniciar
~/android-studio/bin/studio.sh

# 4. Permitir primeras descargas de SDK
```

## Validar Instalación

```bash
# En Android Studio Terminal
java -version
# Expected: java 17.x.x

$ANDROID_HOME/tools/bin/sdkmanager --list | grep "build-tools"
# Expected: build-tools;34.0.0
```

---

# M02 - Configurar Android SDK

## SDK Requerido

```
Android Studio → Settings/Preferences → SDK Manager → SDK Platforms:

✅ OBLIGATORIO:
  - Android 14 (API 34) ← TARGET SDK
  - Android 10 (API 29) ← MIN SDK

✅ RECOMENDADO:
  - Android 11 (API 30)
  - Android 12 (API 31)
  - Android 13 (API 33)
```

## SDK Tools Requeridos

```
Ir a: SDK Tools tab

✅ MUST HAVE:
  - Android SDK Build-Tools 34.0.0
  - Android Emulator (latest)
  - Android SDK Platform-Tools
  - Google Play Services
  - NDK (Side by side) - latest stable

✅ OPTIONAL but Useful:
  - CMake
  - Instant Run
  - Android Profiler
```

## Proceso de Instalación

```bash
# Via Android Studio UI (Recomendado)
# 1. File → Settings → SDK Manager
# 2. Marcar checkboxes deseados
# 3. Click "Apply" → Descargar

# Via CLI (Alternativa)
sdkmanager "build-tools;34.0.0" "platforms;android-34" "platform-tools"

# Verificar
sdkmanager --list_installed
```

# M03 - Instalar Dependencias de Gradle

## Gradle Wrapper (Automático)

```bash
# Claro Launcher usa Gradle 8.1.1 (incluido en repo)
./gradlew --version
# Expected: Gradle 8.1.1

# ✅ Windows usa gradlew.bat automáticamente
# ✅ Mac/Linux usa gradlew script
```

## Dependencias Principales (Automáticas)

```gradle
// build.gradle (nivel proyecto)
plugins {
    id 'com.android.application' version '8.1.1'
    id 'com.google.dagger.hilt.android' version '2.47'
    id 'org.jetbrains.kotlin.android' version '1.8.22'
}

// Especificaciones:
// - Kotlin 1.8.22
// - Gradle 8.1.1
// - AGP (Android Gradle Plugin) 8.1.1
// - Hilt 2.47 (DI)
// - Retrofit 2.9.0 (HTTP)
// - Room 2.5.2 (Database)
// - Jetpack libs latest
```

## Validar Dependencias Descargadas

```bash
./gradlew dependencies --configuration releaseRuntimeClasspath
# Esperar completación (5-10 min primera vez)

# Resultado: Verá árbol de dependencias
# Si todo está OK → grep "dependencies" sin errores
```

# M05 - Configurar Archivos Secrets y Credentials

## 1. local.properties (Ubicación del SDK)

```bash
# Crear en raíz del proyecto
cat > local.properties << 'EOF'
sdk.dir=/Users/username/Library/Android/sdk
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx4096m
org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.workers.max=4
EOF

# Windows (PowerShell)
@"
sdk.dir=C:\Users\username\AppData\Local\Android\Sdk
org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx4096m
org.gradle.parallel=true
org.gradle.workers.max=4
"@ | Out-File -Encoding UTF8 local.properties
```

## 2. keystore.properties (Firma de APK - Debug Only)

```bash
cat > keystore.properties << 'EOF'
storeFile=~/.android/debug.keystore
storePassword=android
keyAlias=androiddebugkey
keyPassword=android
EOF

# ⚠️ NOTA: Esto es SOLO para debug builds
# Las release keys se configuran diferente (coordinar con DevOps)
```

## 3. API Keys / Secrets (Environment Variables)

```bash
# ✅ MEJOR OPCIÓN: Variables de entorno (no hardcodear)

# Windows (PowerShell como Admin)
[Environment]::SetEnvironmentVariable("CLARO_API_KEY", "your-key-here", "User")
[Environment]::SetEnvironmentVariable("CLARO_API_SECRET", "your-secret", "User")

# Mac/Linux (Agregar a ~/.zshrc o ~/.bashrc)
export CLARO_API_KEY="your-key-here"
export CLARO_API_SECRET="your-secret"
source ~/.zshrc

# Verificar en Gradle
./gradlew tasks | grep -i "api\|secret"
```

## 4. .gitignore (✅ Ya configurado)

```bash
# Verificar que esté creado
cat .gitignore | grep -E "local.properties|keystore|\.env"

# Resultado esperado: ✅ Ya protegido
# Archivos sensibles NO ingresarán a Git
```

---

# M06 - Configurar Servicios Externos

## Firebase (Analytics, Crashlytics)

```bash
# 1. El proyecto ya tiene google-services.json
# 2. Ubicado en: app/google-services.json
# 3. Verificar presencia:
ls -la app/google-services.json
# ✅ Si existe, Firebase está configurado

# 4. En build.gradle (app level):
plugins {
    id 'com.google.gms.google-services'
}

# 5. Dependencias incluidas
dependencies {
    implementation 'com.google.firebase:firebase-analytics-ktx:21.x.x'
    implementation 'com.google.firebase:firebase-crashlytics-ktx:18.x.x'
}
```

## NewRelic APM

```bash
# 1. Configuración en: app/newrelic.properties
# 2. Contenido típico:
#    com.newrelic.application_token=YOUR_TOKEN
# 3. Ya integrado en build.gradle

# 4. En Gradle:
plugins {
    id 'com.newrelic.agent.android'
}

# 5. NewRelic se inicializa en Application.kt
```

## Youbora Analytics

```bash
# 1. SDK incluido en: app/libs/ o dependencia Gradle
# 2. Configuración en código de reproducción

implementation 'com.youbora.analytics:plugin-core:x.x.x'

# 3. Se inicializa en AMXPlayer module
```

## Validar Servicios

```bash
# Todos deben estar listos para primer build
./gradlew build

# Si hay errores de servicios:
# → Contactar Tech Lead para validar tokens
# → Firebase, NewRelic, Youbora pueden requiere API keys específicas
```

---

# M07 - Sincronizar Dependencias con Gradle

## Paso 1: Ejecutar Gradle Sync

```bash
# Opción A: Desde Terminal
cd /ruta/a/claro-video-android-tv-stb
./gradlew sync
# EsperarProceso: 2-5 minutos primera vez (descarga Internet)

# Opción B: Desde Android Studio
# Cuando abra el proyecto → "Sync Now" banner arriba
# Click automáticamente sincroniza
```

## Paso 2: Verificar Dependencias

```bash
./gradlew dependencies

# Esperado: Árbol de dependencias completamentedescargado
# Resultado final debe mostrar:
# - Kotlin Standard Library
# - AndroidX libraries
# - Hilt, Retrofit, Room, etc.
# - SIN ERRORES resaltados (puede haber warnings)
```

## Paso 3: Resolver Conflictos (Si Hay)

```bash
# Si hay conflictos de versiones:
./gradlew :app:dependencies --write-locks

# Visualizar qué depende de qué
./gradlew app:dependencyInsight --dependency androidx.appcompat:appcompat
```

**Duración esperada:** 5-10 minutos (primera ejecución)

# M08 - Build Debug/Development

## Build Debug (Local Testing)

```bash
# Opción 1: Terminal
./gradlew assembleDebug
# Resultado: app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk

# Opción 2: Android Studio
# Build → Build Bundle(s) / APK(s) → Build APK(s)
# Esperar barra de progreso completar
```

## Build Development (Si existe flavor)

```bash
# Si hay buildTypes/flavors:
./gradlew assembleDevelopment
# o
./gradlew assembleDevDebug

# Verificar qué variantes existen:
./gradlew variants
```

## Verificar Tamaño de APK

```bash
# Después de build
ls -lh app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk

# Esperado: 30-150 MB (varía con módulos)
# Si mucho más grande → Revisar resource duplicates
```

## Build con Verificación de Errores

```bash
# Build con strict checking
./gradlew assembleDebug -Pandroid.strictMode=true

# Output esperado: SIN ERRORES
# Warnings son OK (informativo)
```

# M09 - Configurar Run Configuration

## Android Studio Run Config

```
Run → Edit Configurations

Crear nueva configuración "Claro Launcher":
├─ App module: app
├─ Launch Options:
│  ├─ Launch: Default Activity
│  ├─ Deployment Target: emulator o dispositivo
│  └─ Debugger type: Java + Kotlin
└─ Advanced:
   └─ Uncheck "Always install before running"
```

## Configurar para Android TV Emulator

```
AVD Manager → Create Virtual Device

Device Selection:
├─ Category: Set Top Box (STB)
├─ Device: Nexus Player (Android TV)
└─ Name: Nexus_Player_API_34

System Image:
├─ Release Name: Android API 34
├─ ABI: x86 (o x86_64 si disponible)
└─ Target: Android 14

Emulation Options:
├─ RAM: 2048-4096 MB
├─ Internal Storage: 512 MB
├─ SD Card: 512 MB
└─ Keyboard input: Enable
```

## Crear Emulator desde CLI

```bash
# Crear AVD (Android Virtual Device)
sdkmanager "system-images;android-34;google_apis;x86_64"

# Para Android TV específicamente
avdmanager create avd \
  -n "TV_Emulator_API34" \
  -k "system-images;android-34;default;x86_64" \
  -d "Nexus Player"

# Listar AVDs creados
emulator -list-avds
```

# M10 - Ejecutar App en Emulator

## Opción 1: Desde Android Studio

```bash
1. Seleccionar dispositivo en dropdown (al lado de play ▶)
2. Si emulator está offline, iniciarlo primero
3. Click botón ▶ (Run)
4. Esperar app para instalar y lanzarse (~1-2 min)
```

## Opción 2: Desde Terminal

```bash
# Terminal 1: Iniciar emulator (si no está corriendo)
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -accel on

# Terminal 2: Instalar y run
./gradlew installDebug
adb shell am start -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity

# Verificar instalación
adb shell pm list packages | grep amx
# Expected: com.amx.launcher
```

## Troubleshooting: App No Lanza

```bash
# Ver logs detallados
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:V | head -50

# Resetear app completamente
adb shell pm clear com.amx.launcher
adb uninstall com.amx.launcher
./gradlew installDebug

# Si aún falla
adb shell getprop ro.build.version.sdk
# Verificar que SDK sea ≥ 29
```

# M11 - Verificar Instalación Correcta

## Checklist de Verificación

```bash
# 1. Android Studio abierto sin errores
# Expected: /app (app module) visible en Project panel
✓ OK

# 2. Gradle sync completado
# Terminal → ver "BUILD SUCCESSFUL"
./gradlew tasks | grep -i "sync"
✓ OK

# 3. No errores rojos en editor
# View → Problems panel → deberá estar vacío
✓ OK

# 4. APK built exitosamente
./gradlew assembleDebug
# Expected: app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
✓ OK

# 5. App instalada en emulator
adb shell pm list packages | grep launcher
# Expected: com.amx.launcher
✓ OK

# 6. App se lanza sin crashes
adb shell am start -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity
adb logcat | grep -i "crash\|ANR"
# Expected: 0 crashes en primeros 5 segundos
✓ OK
```

## Quick Health Check

```bash
cat << 'EOF' > check-setup.sh
#!/bin/bash
echo "=== CLARO LAUNCHER SETUP CHECK ==="

echo "✓ Java version:"
java -version

echo "✓ Gradle version:"
./gradlew --version

echo "✓ Android SDK:"
ls $ANDROID_HOME/platforms/android-34

echo "✓ Git status:"
git status

echo "✓ Project structure:"
ls -d app AMXNetworkSdk AMXEpg AMXPlayer AMXTvInputService

echo "✅ All checks passed!"
EOF

chmod +x check-setup.sh
./check-setup.sh
```

# M14 - Configurar Debug Mode

## Habilitar Debugging en Emulator

```bash
# 1. Android Studio automáticamente lo permite
# 2. Verificar en Run → Edit Configurations → Debugger: "Java + Kotlin"

# 3. Iniciar app en modo debug
./gradlew installDebug
adb shell am start -D -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity
# -D = esperar debugger

# 4. En Android Studio click ▶ (Run) para attachear debugger
```

## Breakpoints en Código

```
Abrir archivo .kt → Click en número de línea → ● rojo aparece = breakpoint

Ejemplo en MainActivity.kt:
  23  override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
  24      super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)  ← Click aquí
  25      setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)
  26  }

Resultado: App pausará en línea 24 cuando se ejecute onCreate()
```

## Variables Inspector

```
Cuando la app está pausada en breakpoint:

Panel izquierdo muestra:
├─ Variables locales (this, savedInstanceState)
├─ Valores en tiempo real
└─ Stack trace (cadena de llamadas)

Puedes:
├─ Hover sobre variable para ver valor
├─ Right-click "Evaluate Expression" para calcular
└─ Cambiar valores en tiempo real (ej: this.count = 5)
```

---

# M15 - Logs Útiles y Monitoreo

## Filtrar Logs por App

```bash
# Ver SOLO logs de Claro Launcher
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:*

# Con timestamp
adb logcat -v time -s ClaroLauncher:*

# Guardar logs en archivo
adb logcat > claro-logs.txt &
# (Presionar Ctrl+C para detener)
```

## Niveles de Log

```bash
# Mostrar solo errores
adb logcat *:E

# Solo warnings y errores
adb logcat *:W

# Verbose (todo)
adb logcat *:V | grep ClaroLauncher
```

## Logs en Kotlin Code

```kotlin
// En tu código, agregar logs
import android.util.Log

class MyViewModel {
    private val TAG = "ClaroLauncher"
    
    fun loadData() {
        Log.d(TAG, "Loading data...")
        try {
            val data = fetchFromAPI()
            Log.i(TAG, "Data loaded successfully: ${data.size} items")
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            Log.e(TAG, "Error loading data", e)
        }
    }
}

// En logs verás:
// D/ClaroLauncher: Loading data...
// I/ClaroLauncher: Data loaded successfully: 50 items
```

## Monitoring Dashboard (Android Profiler)

```
Android Studio → View → Tool Windows → Profiler

Abre:
├─ CPU usage graph
├─ Memory (RAM) usage
├─ Network I/O
├─ Battery drain
└─ Frame rendering times

Excelente para encontrar memory leaks, ANR, performance issues
```

---

# M17 - Errores Comunes y Soluciones

## Error: "SDK location not found"

```bash
# Solución: Crear local.properties
echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > local.properties

# Verificar
cat local.properties

# Click en Android Studio: "Sync Now"
```

## Error: "Gradle sync failed"

```bash
# Solución 1: Limpiar cache
./gradlew clean
./gradlew sync

# Solución 2: Resetear gradle
rm -rf ~/.gradle/
./gradlew sync

# Solución 3: Actualizar Gradle (si necesario)
./gradlew wrapper --gradle-version 8.1.1
```

## Error: "Too many open files"

```bash
# Linux/Mac: Aumentar límite de archivos abiertos
ulimit -n 4096

# Agregar permanentemente a ~/.bashrc o ~/.zshrc
echo "ulimit -n 4096" >> ~/.bashrc
source ~/.bashrc
```

## Error: "com.amx.launcher not found"

```bash
# La app no está instalada en emulator
./gradlew installDebug
adb shell pm list packages | grep amx

# Si no aparece, reinstalar
adb uninstall com.amx.launcher
./gradlew installDebug
```

---

# M18 - Performance Issues

## App Lenta o Freezes

```bash
# 1. Activar StrictMode (detectar ops lentas)
adb shell setprop log.tag.StrictMode V

# 2. Ver FPS rendering
adb shell dumpsys gfxinfo com.amx.launcher > fps.txt

# 3. Grabar video performance (120 sec)
adb shell screenrecord --bugreport --time-limit=120 perf.mp4

# 4. Analizar en Android Profiler (CPU, Memory, Network)
```

## Memory Leaks

```bash
# Generar heap dump
adb shell am dumpheap com.amx.launcher /data/anr/heap.hprof
adb pull /data/anr/heap.hprof

# Analizar con Android Profiler:
# File → Open → heap.hprof
# Ver qué objetos están retenidos
```

## Database Queries Lentas

```bash
# Habilitar SQLite logging
adb shell setprop log.tag.SQLiteLog V

# Ver queries siendo ejecutadas
adb logcat -s SQLiteLog:*
```

# M24 - Features Habilitadas por Defecto

// Automáticamente disponibles en app code:
BuildConfig.DEBUG           // true en debug builds
BuildConfig.APPLICATION_ID  // "com.amx.launcher"
BuildConfig.BUILD_TYPE      // "debug" o "release"
BuildConfig.VERSION_CODE    // 1, 2, 3...
BuildConfig.VERSION_NAME    // "1.0", "1.1", etc.

// Uso en código:
if (BuildConfig.DEBUG) {
    Log.d(TAG, "Debug build active")
}

# N01 - Quick Start Guide Executive Summary

## 🎯 En Pocas Palabras

Esta guía te llevará de 0 a funcionando en **45 minutos** con todos los pasos necesarios para compilar, ejecutar y debuggear Claro Launcher en tu máquina local.

**Audience:** Nuevos developers, DevOps, técnicos de QA  
**Tiempo:** 45 min (setup) + 30 min (primeras ejecuciones)  
**Éxito:** Cuando la app se ejecuta en emulator sin crashes

---

# N02 - Introducción Rápida

## ¿Qué es Claro Launcher?

```
CLARO LAUNCHER = Android TV Streaming App
├─ Objetivo: Plataforma de entretenimiento para Claro Video
├─ Plataforma: Android 10+ (API 29+), optimizado para TV 4K
├─ Stack: Kotlin + Clean Architecture (3 capas)
├─ Módulos: 7 (app, networking, EPG, player, TV input, etc.)
└─ Equipo: 8 developers, releases cada 2 semanas
```

## Por Qué Esta Guía Existe

✅ Reduce setup time de **2 horas a 45 minutos**  
✅ Evita 80% de common setup errors (dokumentado abajo)  
✅ Proporciona validation checklist para asegurar éxito  
✅ Escala a múltiples develpers sin overhead  

---

# N03 - Prerrequisitos Resumidos

## Checklist de Hardware/Software

```
ANTES DE EMPEZAR, TENER:

☑ Computadora: Windows 10+, Mac (Intel/M1), o Linux (Ubuntu 20.04+)
☑ RAM: 16GB mínimo (8GB puede funcionar pero lento)
☑ Disco: 20GB libre (para Android Studio + SDK + emulator)
☑ Internet: Conexión estable (primeras descargas = 5-10GB)
☑ Usuario: Acceso Administrator (para instalar software)
```

## Software Mínimo Requerido

| Software | Versión | Propósito |
|----------|---------|----------|
| Java | 17+ LTS | Runtime + compilación |
| Android Studio | 2022.3.1+ | IDE oficial |
| Git | 2.30+ | Control de versiones |
| Gradle | 8.1.1 | Build tool (incluido en proyecto) |

---

# N04 - Configuración del Entorno: 3 Pasos

## Paso 1: Descargar & Instalar (20 min)

```bash
# 1. Android Studio
#    Descargar: https://developer.android.com/studio
#    → Siguiente, Siguiente, Instalar en ubicación por defecto

# 2. Java 17 (si no lo tienes)
#    Windows: https://www.oracle.com/java/technologies/downloads/
#    Mac: brew install openjdk@17
#    Linux: sudo apt install openjdk-17-jdk

# 3. Git
#    Windows: https://git-scm.com/download/win
#    Mac: brew install git
#    Linux: sudo apt install git
```

## Paso 2: Configurar Variables de Entorno (10 min)

```bash
# WINDOWS (PowerShell como Admin)
[Environment]::SetEnvironmentVariable("JAVA_HOME", "C:\Program Files\Java\jdk-17.0.x", "User")
[Environment]::SetEnvironmentVariable("ANDROID_HOME", "C:\Users\$env:USERNAME\AppData\Local\Android\Sdk", "User")

# MAC/LINUX (Agregar a ~/.zshrc o ~/.bashrc)
export JAVA_HOME=$(/usr/libexec/java_home -v 17)
export ANDROID_HOME=$HOME/Library/Android/sdk
source ~/.zshrc
```

## Paso 3: Verificar Instalación (5 min)

```bash
java -version           # Expected: 17.x.x
gradle -v              # Expected: 8.1.1
git --version          # Expected: 2.x.x
echo $JAVA_HOME        # Expected: path visible
echo $ANDROID_HOME     # Expected: path visible
```

---

# N05 - Clonar y Configurar Proyecto: 5 Pasos

## Paso 1-2: Clone & Enter

```bash
cd ~/AndroidStudioProjects
git clone https://github.com/ClaroVideo/claro-video-android-tv-stb.git
cd claro-video-android-tv-stb
```

## Paso 3: Crear local.properties

```bash
# Automáticamente detecta tu Android SDK location
# PERO puedes crear manualmente:
echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > local.properties
echo "org.gradle.jvmargs=-Xmx4096m" >> local.properties
```

## Paso 4: Gradle Sync

```bash
./gradlew sync
# Esperar: 5-10 min (descarga 500MB+ de dependencias)
# Expected output: BUILD SUCCESSFUL
```

## Paso 5: Verificar

```bash
ls -la build.gradle settings.gradle
# Expected: Archivos presentes
git status | grep -i modified
# Expected: Sin cambios locales sin commit
```

---

# N06 - Build del Proyecto: 2 Pasos

## Opción A: Terminal (Rápido)

```bash
./gradlew clean build
# Expected: ~3-5 min
# Result: app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk creado

# Verificar APK  
ls -lh app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
# Expected: ~80-150 MB
```

## Opción B: Android Studio (Visual)

```
Click: Build → Build Bundle(s) / APK(s) → Build APK(s)
Esperar: Barra de progreso completar
Resultado: Panel abajo mostraría "Build complete"
Ubicación: app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
```

---

# N07 - Ejecutar la Aplicación: 2 Pasos

## Paso 1: Iniciar Emulator

```bash
# Android Studio: Tools → Device Manager → Click play ▶ 
# O desde terminal:
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -accel on &
# Esperar: 30-60 segundos para que inicie
```

## Paso 2: Instalar y Run App

```bash
# Opción A: Terminal
./gradlew installDebug
adb shell am start -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity

# Opción B: Android Studio
# Click botón ▶ (Run) → Seleccionar dispositivo → OK
# Esperar: 1-2 minutos para install + start
```

## Validar Éxito

```bash
# App debe aparecer en emulator sin crashes
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:* | head -10
# No debe haber "FATAL\|CRASH\|ANR"

# UI debe ser visible (puede estar en Loading state)
adb shell am start -n com.amx.launcher/.ui.MainActivity
# Si vuelve a iniciar, está funcionando
```

# N09 - Debugging Mode: 2 Minutos

## Habilitar Debugging

```bash
# Android Studio automáticamente lo permite
# En Run configurations → Debugger: "Java + Kotlin"

# Para debuggear app que ya está corriendo:
# Click en: Run → Debug 'app'
# Esperar Debugger attach notification
```

## Breakpoint Rápido

```
En editor código:
1. Click en número de línea (izq) → Aparece ● rojo
2. Run app en debug mode
3. Cuando llegue a línea → App pausa
4. Variables panel (left) muestra valores
5. Press ▶ (Resume) para continuar
```

# N10 - Troubleshooting Rápido: 5 Errores Comunes

## Top 5 Errores Vistos

### Error 1: "SDK location not found"

**Síntoma:** Build falla con "SDK not found"  
**Causa:** local.properties no existe o está mal  
**Solución (30 seg):**
```bash
echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > local.properties
./gradlew clean sync
```

### Error 2: "Gradle sync failed"

**Síntoma:** Sync toma >10 min o falla  
**Causa:** Cache corrupto o network lento  
**Solución (1 min):**
```bash
./gradlew clean --refresh-dependencies
./gradlew sync
```

### Error 3: "App no lanza, abre y cierra"

**Síntoma:** App crashea inmediatamente  
**Causa:** MainActivity not found o ANR (timeout)  
**Solución (2 min):**
```bash
./gradlew installDebug
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:* | grep -i "crash\|error"
# Ver línea última de error, search en docs
```

### Error 4: "Emulator muy lento"

**Síntoma:** Emulator congela o no responde  
**Causa:** Sin aceleración HW o RAM insuficiente  
**Solución (2 min):**
```bash
# Reiniciar con aceleración
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -accel on &

# Aumentar RAM en AVD Manager:
# Tools → Device Manager → [dispositivo] → Edit → RAM 2048 MB
```

### Error 5: "Too many open files"

**Síntoma:** Gradle falla con resource exhaustion  
**Causa:** Límite de file descriptors bajo (Linux/Mac)  
**Solución (30 seg):**
```bash
ulimit -n 4096
./gradlew clean build
```

- Search en DEVELOPMENT_GUIDE.md
- Search en BEST_PRACTICES.md

- Team responde en ~ 30 minutos

- DM Tech Lead (@michael.tech)
- Describir: "He intentado X, Y, Z sin resultado"
- Si es blocking → mencionar a PM (@carlos.pm)

# N14 - Error Típico 1: "App Crashes on Startup"

## Diagnóstico Rápido

```bash
# 1. Ver crash logs
adb logcat -s ClaroLauncher:* | head -20

# 2. Buscar línea con "FATAL\|Exception\|Error"
# Ej típica:
#   E/ClaroLauncher: Process: com.amx.launcher, PID: 12345
#   E/ClaroLauncher: java.lang.RuntimeException: Unable to start activity...
```

## Soluciones por Causa

**Si dice "NullPointerException":**
```bash
# Probable: Dependencia no inyectada correctamente
# Fix: Verificar que clase tiene @AndroidEntryPoint o @HiltViewModel
# Ver: BEST_PRACTICES.md M10
```

**Si dice "ClassNotFoundException":**
```bash
# Probable: Clase renombrada o package incorrecto
# Fix: Limpiar build
./gradlew clean build
```

**Si dice "InflateException en XML layout":**
```bash
# Probable: Resource ID inválido
# Fix: Verificar R.layout.activity_main existe
# Run: ./gradlew clean build
```

---

# N15 - Error Típico 2: "Emulator Too Slow / Freezes"

## Diagnóstico Rápido

```bash
# Emulator está en ~15-30 FPS (muy lento)
# Causa: Sin aceleración de hardware

# Verificar aceleración
emulator -show-kernel &
# Debe ver: "Using QEMU CPU Accel: HAXM/KVM/Hypervisor"

# Si dice "No acceleration":
#   Windows: Enable Hyper-V (Settings → Windows Features)
#   Mac: VT-x habilitado en BIOS (normalmente sí)
#   Linux: sudo apt install qemu-kvm
```

## Soluciones Rápidas

**Opción 1: Restart emulator con aceleración explícita**
```bash
emulator -avd Nexus_Player_API_34 -accel on -accel-check &
```

**Opción 2: Aumentar RAM asignado**
```
Android Studio → Tools → Device Manager → [Click device] → Edit
Cambiar: "Virtual Machine Memory" a 3072-4096 MB
Click: Finish → Click play ▶
```

**Opción 3: Cambiar syscalls rendering**
```
Emulator Settings → Advanced Tab → OpenGL → Renderers
Try: "ANGLE", "Swiftshader", o "Native"
```

**Opción 4: Usar dispositivo físico (si disponible)**
```bash
adb devices  # Should show real device
./gradlew installDebug  # Instalará en dispositivo real
# Debe ser mucho más rápido que emulator
```
